We now give a description of the object type theory. This is a simple
type theory with guarded recursion that can be seen as a variant of
Atkey and McBride's type system \cite{atkey2013productive} but
allowing the presence of at most one clock in context.
In Atkey and McBride's system, judgements are parametrized by a clock
context. In our case, the clock context can either be empty or contain
a single clock \IC{Œ∫}.

\begin{code}%
\>[0]\AgdaKeyword{data}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{ClockContext}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaPrimitiveType{Set}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaKeyword{where}\<%
\\
\>[0][@{}l@{\AgdaIndent{0}}]%
\>[2]\AgdaInductiveConstructor{‚àÖ}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{ClockContext}\<%
\\
%
\>[2]\AgdaInductiveConstructor{Œ∫}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{ClockContext}\<%
\end{code}

\AgdaHide{
\begin{code}%
\>[0]\AgdaKeyword{mutual}\<%
\end{code}
}

Types depend on a clock context. 

\begin{AgdaAlign}
\begin{code}%
\>[0][@{}l@{\AgdaIndent{1}}]%
\>[2]\AgdaKeyword{data}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{ClockContext}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaPrimitiveType{Set}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaKeyword{where}\<%
\end{code}

We have the unit type which exists only in the empty clock context. We
have products, coproducts and function spaces which exist in all clock
contexts.

\begin{code}%
\>[2][@{}l@{\AgdaIndent{1}}]%

\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaBound{Œî}\<%
\end{code}

In addition to the usual simple type formers, there are types that
allow us to specify guarded recursive and coinductive types. We have
the later modality, which takes a type in the \IC{Œ∫} clock context and
returns a type in the \IC{Œ∫} clock context.
We have clock quantification, which takes a type in the \IC{Œ∫} clock
context and returns a type in the \IC{‚àÖ} clock context. We also have a
weakening type former, which embeds any type in the \IC{‚àÖ} clock context
into types in the \IC{Œ∫} clock context.

\begin{code}%
%
\>[4]\AgdaInductiveConstructor{later}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{Œ∫}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{Œ∫}\<%
\\
%
\>[4]\AgdaInductiveConstructor{clock{-}q}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{Œ∫}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{‚àÖ}\<%
\\
%
\>[4]\AgdaInductiveConstructor{weakenT}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{‚àÖ}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaInductiveConstructor{Œ∫}\<%
\end{code}

Finally we have guarded recursive types which exist in all clock
contexts.

\end{code}
\end{AgdaAlign}

A guarded recursive type in a clock context \Ar{Œî} takes an element of
\F{Poly} \Ar{Œî} as its input. We call these elements polynomials.

We can associate to each polynomial \Ar{P} an endofunctor \F{evalP}
\Ar{P} on \F{Type} \Ar{Œî}. Then \IC{Œº} \Ar{P} is the least fixed point
of \F{evalP} \Ar{P}. For this fixpoint to exist, one typically
restricts the constructors of the type family \F{Poly} so that the
functor \F{evalP} \Ar{P} is strictly positive, for all \Ar{P}.  Here
we consider a grammar for polynomials consisting of constant functors,
the identity functor, products, coproducts and the later
modality. Exponentials with constant domain and clock quantification
could also be added to the grammar, but we did not consider them in
our formalization.  Because of the presence of constant functors in
the grammar, the type family \F{Poly} has to be defined simultaneously
with \F{Type}.

\begin{code}%
\>[0]\AgdaFunction{evalP}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{:}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚àÄ}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{\{}\AgdaBound{Œî}\AgdaSymbol{\}}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Poly}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaBound{Œî}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaBound{Œî}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaSymbol{‚Üí}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaDatatype{Type}\AgdaSpace{}%
\AgdaBound{Œî}\<%
\end{code}

\AgdaHide{
